### Sale of tobacco etc

Prospective

#### 52Age of sale for tobacco products etc

(1\)The Tobacco and Primary Medical Services (Scotland) Act [2010 (asp 3\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/asp/2010/3) is amended as follows.


(2\)In section 4 (sale of tobacco products to persons under 18\)—


(a)in subsection (1\), for “under the age of 18” substitute “born on or after 1 January 2009”;


(b)in subsection (2\)(a), for “under the age of 18 (“the customer”) to be aged 18 or over” substitute “born on or after 1 January 2009 (“the customer”) to have been born before that date”;


(c)after subsection (5\) insert—


“(6\)In this section “sell” means sell by retail.”;


(d)in the heading, for “under 18” substitute “born on or after 1 January 2009”.


(3\)In section 4B (age verification policy)—


(a)for subsection (3\) substitute—


“(3\)An “age verification policy”—


(a)in relation to a tobacco business or herbal smoking product business, is a policy that steps are to be taken to establish the age of a person attempting to buy a tobacco product, herbal smoking product or cigarette papers on the premises (the “customer”) if it appears to the person selling the tobacco product, herbal smoking product or cigarette papers that the customer may have been born on or after 1 January 2009 (or such earlier date as may be specified in the policy);


(b)in relation to a vaping product business or nicotine product business, is a policy that steps are to be taken to establish the age of a person attempting to buy a vaping product, or a nicotine product, on the premises (the “customer”) if it appears to the person selling the product that the customer may be under the age of 25 (or such older age as may be specified in the policy).


(3A)In relation to times before the end of 2033, the reference in [subsection (3\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p03348)[(a)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p03351) to the customer being born on or after 1 January 2009 (or such earlier date as may be specified in the policy) has effect as a reference to the customer being under the age of 25 (or such older age as may be specified in the policy).”;


(b)in subsection (4\), for “(3\)” substitute “[(3\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-52-3)[(b)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-52-3-b)”.


(4\)In section 6 (purchase of tobacco products on behalf of persons under 18\)—


(a)in subsection (1\), for “under the age of 18” substitute “born on or after 1 January 2009”;


(b)in the heading, for “under 18” substitute “born on or after 1 January 2009”.


(5\)In section 8 (display of warning statements), in subsection (2\)(a), for “under the age of 18” substitute “born on or after 1 January 2009”.

### Snus etc

#### 58Ban on manufacture of snus etc

After section 9 of the Tobacco and Primary Medical Services (Scotland) Act [2010 (asp 3\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/asp/2010/3) insert—


##### “Snus etc

###### 9ABan on manufacture of snus etc

(1\)It is an offence to manufacture a relevant oral tobacco product.


(2\)In subsection [(1\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p03576) “relevant oral tobacco product” means a tobacco product that—


(a)is intended for oral use,


(b)is not intended to be inhaled or chewed, and


(c)consists wholly or partly of tobacco in powder or particulate form.


(3\)A person guilty of an offence under this section is liable—


(a)on summary conviction, to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 12 months, or a fine not exceeding the statutory maximum, or both;


(b)on conviction on indictment, to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 2 years, or a fine, or both.”


Commencement Information

I71S. 58 in force at 29\.9\.2026, see [**s. 175(1\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/1)

#### 59Ban on sales of snus etc

After section [9A](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p03527) of the Tobacco and Primary Medical Services (Scotland) Act [2010 (asp 3\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/asp/2010/3) (inserted by section [58](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-58) of this Act) insert—


##### “9BBan on sales of snus etc

(1\)It is an offence to—


(a)sell a relevant oral tobacco product, or


(b)offer or expose a relevant oral tobacco product for sale.


(2\)In subsection [(1\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p03576) “relevant oral tobacco product” has the meaning given by section [9A](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p03527)[(2\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p03533).


(3\)It is a defence for a person charged with an offence under this section to prove that they took all reasonable steps to avoid the commission of the offence.


(4\)A person guilty of an offence under this section is liable—


(a)on summary conviction, to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 12 months, or a fine not exceeding the statutory maximum, or both;


(b)on conviction on indictment, to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 2 years, or a fine, or both.”


Commencement Information

I72S. 59 in force at 29\.9\.2026, see [**s. 175(1\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/1)

#### 60Possession of snus etc with intent to supply

(1\)After section [9B](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p03574) of the Tobacco and Primary Medical Services (Scotland) Act [2010 (asp 3\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/asp/2010/3) (inserted by section [59](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-59) of this Act) insert—


##### “9CPossession of snus etc with intent to supply

(1\)It is an offence for a person to have a relevant oral tobacco product in their possession with intent to supply it to another in the course of business.


(2\)In subsection [(1\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p03576) “relevant oral tobacco product” has the meaning given by section [9A](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p03527)[(2\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p03533).


(3\)A person guilty of an offence under this section is liable—


(a)on summary conviction, to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 12 months, or a fine not exceeding the statutory maximum, or both;


(b)on conviction on indictment, to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 2 years, or a fine, or both.”

### Vaping and nicotine products

#### 61Extension of offences to vaping and nicotine products

(1\)The Tobacco and Primary Medical Services (Scotland) Act [2010 (asp 3\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/asp/2010/3) is amended in accordance with subsections [(2\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-61-2) to [(7\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-61-7).


(2\)In the italic heading before section 4, for “and nicotine vapour” substitute “, vaping and nicotine”.


(3\)In section 4A (sale of nicotine vapour products to persons under 18\)—


(a)in subsection (1\), for “nicotine vapour” substitute “vaping product or nicotine”;


(b)in the heading, for “nicotine vapour” substitute “vaping and nicotine”.


(4\)In section 4B (age verification policy)—


(a)in subsection (1\)(a) and (b), for “tobacco or nicotine vapour product business” substitute “relevant business”;


(b)after subsection (1\) insert—


“(1A)In this section “relevant business” means a business which involves the sale of one or more of the following by retail—


(a)tobacco products;


(b)herbal smoking products;


(c)vaping products;


(d)nicotine products.”;


(c)for subsection (2\) substitute—


“(2\)Subsection (1\) does not apply in relation to premises from which—


(a)a product mentioned in subsection (1A) or cigarette papers are, in pursuance of a sale, despatched for delivery to different premises, and


(b)no other relevant business is carried on.”;


(d)in subsection (3\)—


(i)for “tobacco product, cigarette papers or a nicotine vapour product” substitute “product mentioned in subsection [(1A)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p03690) or cigarette papers”;


(ii)for “the tobacco product, cigarette papers or nicotine vapour product” substitute “the product”;


(e)in subsection (5\)(b) and (c), for “tobacco product, cigarette papers or a nicotine vapour product” substitute “product mentioned in subsection [(1A)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p03690) or cigarette papers”;


(f)in subsection (6\), for “tobacco or nicotine vapour product business” substitute “relevant business”.


(5\)In section 4C (sale of tobacco or nicotine vapour products by persons under 18\)—


(a)in subsection (1\), for “or a nicotine vapour” substitute “, a vaping product or a nicotine”;


(b)in the heading, for “or nicotine vapour” substitute “, vaping or nicotine”.


(6\)In section 6A (purchase of nicotine vapour products on behalf of persons under 18\)—


(a)in subsection (1\), for “nicotine vapour” substitute “vaping or nicotine”;


(b)in the heading for “nicotine vapour” substitute “vaping or nicotine”.


(7\)For section 9 substitute—


##### “Vending machines

###### 9Prohibited vending machines

(1\)A person who has the management or control of premises on which a prohibited vending machine is available for use commits an offence.


(2\)A person guilty of an offence under [subsection (1\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p03786) is liable on summary conviction to a fine not exceeding level 4 on the standard scale.


(3\)In this section, “prohibited vending machine” means a machine from which any of the following products may be bought or from which they are dispensed to a customer in connection with a sale—


(a)tobacco products;


(b)herbal smoking products;


(c)cigarette papers;


(d)vaping products;


(e)nicotine products.”


(8\)In the Health (Tobacco, Nicotine etc. and Care) (Scotland) Act [2016 (asp 14\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/asp/2016/14) omit section 7 (power to extend vending machine prohibition).


Commencement Information

I74S. 61 in force at 29\.9\.2026, see [**s. 175(1\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/1)

#### 62Meaning of “nicotine product”

Before section 36 of the Tobacco and Primary Medical Services (Scotland) Act [2010 (asp 3\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/asp/2010/3) insert—


##### “35BMeaning of “nicotine product” in this Part

(1\)In this Part, a “nicotine product” is—


(a)a device which is intended to enable nicotine to be delivered into the human body,


(b)an item which is intended to form part of a device within paragraph [(a)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-51-1-a),


(c)nicotine, or any substance containing nicotine, which is intended to be delivered into the human body, or


(d)an item containing anything within paragraph [(c)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-51-1-c).


(2\)But the following are not nicotine products—


(a)a tobacco product;


(b)a smoking related product;


(c)a herbal smoking product;


(d)any device which is intended to be used for the consumption of tobacco products or herbal smoking products;


(e)a vaping product;


(f)a medicinal product;


(g)a medical device.”


Commencement Information

I75S. 62 in force at 29\.9\.2026, see [**s. 175(1\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/1)

### Displays of products or prices

#### 64Displays of vaping and nicotine products

(1\)The Tobacco and Primary Medical Services (Scotland) Act [2010 (asp 3\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/asp/2010/3) is amended as follows.


(2\)After section 3 insert—


##### “3ADisplay of products or prices

(1\)The Scottish Ministers may by regulations impose prohibitions, requirements or limitations on retailers in relation to—


(a)the display, in the course of business, of relevant products in a place where those products are offered for sale;


(b)the display, in the course of business, of empty retail packaging of relevant products in a place where those products are offered for sale;


(c)the display, in the course of business, of prices of relevant products in a place where those products are offered for sale.


(2\)In subsection [(1\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-13-1) “relevant products” means—


(a)herbal smoking products,


(b)vaping products, or


(c)nicotine products.


(3\)In subsection [(1\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-13-1)[(a)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-13-1-a) a reference to a product includes anything that represents the product and that is intended to be exchanged for it at the point of sale.


(4\)Regulations under this section may create offences in relation to a failure to comply with the regulations.


(5\)The regulations must provide for any offence to be triable summarily and punishable with a fine not exceeding level 4 on the standard scale.


(6\)For the purposes of subsection [(1\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-13-1), a website is not a place.


(7\)Before making regulations under this section the Scottish Ministers must consult any persons they consider it appropriate to consult.”


(3\)In each of the following provisions after “Chapter 1 or 2” insert “or any regulations made under those Chapters”—


<ul><li><p>section 15(3)(d) and (4)(b);
</p></li><li><p>section 16(3)(a);
</p></li><li><p>section 26(2)(a);
</p></li><li><p>section 27(1);
</p></li><li><p>section 32(1) and (4).
</p></li></ul>

(4\)In section 26(2\)(b), after “Chapters” insert “or any regulations made under those Chapters”.


(5\)In section 33 (presumption as to contents of container), in subsection (1\), at the end insert “or under regulations made under section [3A](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p03957)”.


(6\)In section 34 (offences by bodies corporate etc), in subsection (1\)(a), after “this Act” insert “or regulations made under it”.


(7\)In section 40 (orders and regulations), in subsection (4\), at the appropriate place insert—


<ul><li><p><span><span>“</span>section </span><a href="https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p03957"><span>3A</span></a><a href="https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p03959"><span>(1)<span>”</span>.</span></a>
</p></li></ul>

Commencement Information

I77S. 64 in force at Royal Assent for specified purposes, see [**s. 175(2\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/2)

### Free distribution and discounts

#### 65Free distribution and discount of products

(1\)In the Tobacco and Primary Medical Services (Scotland) Act [2010 (asp 3\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/asp/2010/3), after section 8 insert—


##### “Free distribution etc

###### 8AFree distribution and discount of products

(1\)A person commits an offence if—


(a)the person—


(i)gives away a product or coupon to a member of the public or sells by retail a product or coupon at a substantial discount, or


(ii)causes or permits that to happen, and


(b)either—


(i)their purpose in doing so is to promote a relevant product, or


(ii)the effect of their doing so will be to promote a relevant product and they know, or have reason to suspect, that will be the effect.


(2\)In subsection [(1\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04897) “relevant product” means—


(a)a tobacco product,


(b)a herbal smoking product,


(c)a smoking related product,


(d)a vaping product, or


(e)a nicotine product.


(3\)A person who commits an offence under this section is liable—


(a)on summary conviction, to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 12 months, or a fine not exceeding the statutory maximum, or both;


(b)on conviction on indictment, to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 2 years, or a fine, or both.


(4\)In this section “coupon” means anything (whether in physical or electronic form) which, by itself or together with something else, can be redeemed for a product or service or for cash or any other benefit.


###### 8BFree distribution of products: defences

(1\)Where a person is charged with an offence under section [8A](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04073) of giving away a vaping product or nicotine product, or a coupon for such a product, it is a defence for the person to prove that the product or coupon was given away in accordance with arrangements made by a public authority.


(2\)The Scottish Ministers may by regulations create further defences to the offence under section [8A](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04073) of giving away a vaping product or nicotine product or a coupon for such a product.


(3\)Regulations under this section may amend this Part.”


(2\)In section 40 of that Act (orders and regulations), in subsection (4\), at the appropriate place insert—


<ul><li><p><span><span>“</span>section </span><a href="https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04145"><span>8B<span>”</span>.</span></a>
</p></li></ul>

(3\)In the Health (Tobacco, Nicotine etc. and Care) (Scotland) Act 2016 omit section 18\.


Commencement Information

I79S. 65 in force at Royal Assent for specified purposes, see [**s. 175(2\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/2)

I80S. 65 in force at 29\.9\.2026 in so far as not already in force, see [**s. 175(1\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/1)

#### 71Power to extend 2010 Act to other products

(1\)The Tobacco and Primary Medical Services (Scotland) Act [2010 (asp 3\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/asp/2010/3) is amended as follows.


(2\)After section 34 insert—


##### “34APower to extend this Part to other products

(1\)The Scottish Ministers may by regulations amend this Part for the purpose of extending any provision that applies in relation to a tobacco product to—


(a)a device of a specified description which enables a tobacco product to be consumed otherwise than by being smoked (for example, a heated tobacco device);


(b)an item which is intended to form part of such a device.


(2\)Before making regulations under this section the Scottish Ministers must consult any persons they consider it appropriate to consult.


(3\)The Scottish Ministers may by regulations amend this Part for the purpose of extending any provision that applies in relation to a tobacco product to—


(a)some or all smoking related products;


(b)if not falling within paragraph (a), a filter that does not form part of a tobacco product or herbal smoking product.


(4\)The Scottish Ministers may by regulations amend this Part for the purpose of extending to filters any provision made by sections [9A](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p03527) to [9C](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p03623) in relation to a relevant oral tobacco product.”


(3\)In section 40 (orders and regulations), in subsection (4\), at the appropriate place insert—


<ul><li><p><span><span>“</span>section </span><a href="https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04254"><span>34A<span>”</span>.</span></a>

Part 3Sale and distribution: Northern Ireland
---------------------------------------------

### Sale of tobacco etc

#### 72Age of sale for tobacco products etc

For Article 3 of the Health and Personal Social Services (Northern Ireland) Order 1978 ([S.I. 1978/1907 (N.I. 26\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/nisi/1978/1907)) substitute—


##### “3Sale of tobacco etc

(1\)It is an offence to sell any of the following to a person born on or after 1 January 2009—


(a)a tobacco product;


(b)a herbal smoking product;


(c)cigarette papers.


(2\)It is a defence for a person charged with an offence under this Article to prove—


(a)that they took such steps as may be specified in regulations made by the Department to verify that the customer was born before 1 January 2009, or


(b)that they otherwise took all reasonable steps to avoid the commission of the offence.


(3\)Regulations may not be made by the Department under paragraph [(2\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04334)[(a)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04337) unless a draft of the regulations has been laid before and approved by a resolution of the Assembly.


(4\)A person guilty of an offence under this Article is liable on summary conviction to a fine not exceeding level 5 on the standard scale.”


Commencement Information

I88S. 72 in force at Royal Assent for specified purposes, see [**s. 175(2\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/2)

I89S. 72 in force at 1\.1\.2027 in so far as not already in force, see [**s. 175(3\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/3)

Prospective

#### 73Purchase of tobacco on behalf of others

For Article 4A of the Health and Personal Social Services (Northern Ireland) Order 1978 ([S.I. 1978/1907 (N.I. 26\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/nisi/1978/1907)) substitute—


##### “4APurchase of tobacco etc on behalf of persons born on or after 1 January 2009

(1\)It is an offence for a person aged 18 or over to buy, or attempt to buy, any of the following on behalf of a person born on or after 1 January 2009—


(a)a tobacco product;


(b)a herbal smoking product;


(c)cigarette papers.


(2\)It is a defence for a person charged with an offence under this Article to prove that they had no reason to suspect that the other person was born on or after 1 January 2009\.


(3\)It is a defence for a person charged with an offence under this Article in respect of cigarette papers to prove that they had no reason to suspect that the other person intended to use the papers for smoking.


(4\)A person guilty of an offence under this Article is liable on summary conviction to a fine not exceeding level 5 on the standard scale.”


Commencement Information

I90S. 73 in force at 1\.1\.2027, see [**s. 175(3\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/3)

Prospective

#### 74Tobacco vending machines

After Article [4A](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04366) of the Health and Personal Social Services (Northern Ireland) Order 1978 ([S.I. 1978/1907 (N.I. 26\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/nisi/1978/1907)) (inserted by section [73](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-73) of this Act) insert—


##### “4BTobacco vending machines

(1\)A person commits an offence if the person has the management or control of premises on which a tobacco vending machine is available for use.


(2\)A person guilty of an offence under this Article is liable on summary conviction to a fine not exceeding level 5 on the standard scale.


(3\)In this Article “tobacco vending machine” means a machine from which any of the following products may be bought or from which they are dispensed to a customer in connection with a sale—


(a)tobacco products,


(b)herbal smoking products, or


(c)cigarette papers.”


Commencement Information

I91S. 74 in force at 29\.9\.2026, see [**s. 175(1\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/1)

Prospective

#### 75Sale of unpackaged cigarettes

After Article [4B](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04407) of the Health and Personal Social Services (Northern Ireland) Order 1978 ([S.I. 1978/1907 (N.I. 26\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/nisi/1978/1907)) (inserted by section [74](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-74) of this Act) insert—


##### “4CSale of unpackaged cigarettes

(1\)It is an offence for a tobacco retailer to sell cigarettes that are not in their original packaging.


(2\)A person guilty of an offence under this Article is liable on summary conviction to a fine not exceeding level 3 on the standard scale.


(3\)In this Article “original packaging” means the retail packaging in which the cigarettes were supplied to the tobacco retailer for the purpose of sale.”


Commencement Information

I92S. 75 in force at 29\.9\.2026, see [**s. 175(1\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/1)

#### 76Age of sale notice at point of sale

After Article [4C](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04444) of the Health and Personal Social Services (Northern Ireland) Order 1978 ([S.I. 1978/1907 (N.I. 26\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/nisi/1978/1907)) (inserted by section [75](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-75) of this Act) insert—


##### “4DAge of sale notice at point of sale

(1\)A tobacco retailer must display an age of sale notice at any premises at which they sell tobacco products.


(2\)For the purposes of this Article an “age of sale notice” is a notice containing the following statement—


“It is illegal to sell tobacco products to anyone born on or after 1 January 2009”.


(3\)The notice must be displayed in a prominent position where it is readily visible to people at each point of sale of tobacco products.


(4\)The notice must comply with any requirements set out in regulations made by the Department as to the size or appearance of—


(a)the statement on the notice, or


(b)any other aspect of the notice.


(5\)Regulations under paragraph [(4\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04489) are subject to negative resolution.


(6\)A person who fails to display an age of sale notice as required by this Article commits an offence.


(7\)It is a defence for a person charged with an offence under this Article to prove that they took all reasonable steps to avoid the commission of the offence.


(8\)A person guilty of an offence under this Article is liable on summary conviction to a fine not exceeding level 3 on the standard scale.”


Commencement Information

I93S. 76 in force at Royal Assent for specified purposes, see [**s. 175(2\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/2)

I94S. 76 in force at 1\.1\.2027 in so far as not already in force, see [**s. 175(3\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/3)

Prospective

### Snus etc

#### 77Ban on manufacture of snus etc

After Article [4D](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04469) of the Health and Personal Social Services (Northern Ireland) Order 1978 ([S.I. 1978/1907 (N.I. 26\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/nisi/1978/1907)) (inserted by section [76](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-76) of this Act) insert—


##### “Snus etc

###### 4EBan on manufacture of snus etc

(1\)It is an offence to manufacture a relevant oral tobacco product.


(2\)In paragraph [(1\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-8-1) “relevant oral tobacco product” means a tobacco product that—


(a)is intended for oral use,


(b)is not intended to be inhaled or chewed, and


(c)consists wholly or partly of tobacco in powder or particulate form.


(3\)A person guilty of an offence under this Article is liable—


(a)on summary conviction, to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 6 months, or a fine not exceeding the statutory maximum, or both;


(b)on conviction on indictment, to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 2 years, or a fine, or both.”


Commencement Information

I95S. 77 in force at 29\.9\.2026, see [**s. 175(1\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/1)

#### 78Ban on sales of snus etc

After Article [4E](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04532) of the Health and Personal Social Services (Northern Ireland) Order 1978 ([S.I. 1978/1907 (N.I. 26\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/nisi/1978/1907)) (inserted by section [77](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-77) of this Act) insert—


##### “4FBan on sales of snus etc

(1\)It is an offence to—


(a)sell a relevant oral tobacco product, or


(b)offer or expose a relevant oral tobacco product for sale.


(2\)In paragraph (1\) “relevant oral tobacco product” has the meaning given by Article [4E](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04532)[(2\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04538).


(3\)It is a defence for a person charged with an offence under this Article to prove that they took all reasonable steps to avoid the commission of the offence.


(4\)A person guilty of an offence under this Article is liable—


(a)on summary conviction, to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 6 months, or a fine not exceeding the statutory maximum, or both;


(b)on conviction on indictment, to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 2 years, or a fine, or both.”


Commencement Information

I96S. 78 in force at 29\.9\.2026, see [**s. 175(1\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/1)

#### 79Possession of snus etc with intent to supply

(1\)After Article [4F](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04579) of the Health and Personal Social Services (Northern Ireland) Order 1978 ([S.I. 1978/1907 (N.I. 26\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/nisi/1978/1907)) (inserted by section [78](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-78) of this Act) insert—


##### “4GPossession of snus etc with intent to supply

(1\)It is an offence for a person to have a relevant oral tobacco product in their possession with intent to supply it to another in the course of business.


(2\)In paragraph (1\) “relevant oral tobacco product” has the meaning given by Article [4E](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04532)[(2\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04538).


(3\)A person guilty of an offence under this Article is liable—


(a)on summary conviction, to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 6 months, or a fine not exceeding the statutory maximum, or both;


(b)on conviction on indictment, to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 2 years, or a fine, or both.”


Commencement Information

I97S. 79 in force at 29\.9\.2026, see [**s. 175(1\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/1)

### Vaping and nicotine products

#### 80Sale of vaping or nicotine products to under 18s

After Article [4G](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04627) of Health and Personal Social Services (Northern Ireland) Order 1978 ([S.I. 1978/1907 (N.I. 26\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/nisi/1978/1907)) (inserted by section [79](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-79) of this Act) insert—


##### “Vaping and nicotine products

###### 4HSale of vaping or nicotine products to under 18s

(1\)It is an offence to sell a vaping product or nicotine product to a person who is under the age of 18\.


(2\)It is a defence for a person charged with an offence under this Article to prove—


(a)that they took such steps as may be specified in regulations made by the Department to verify that the customer was at least 18 years old, or


(b)that they otherwise took all reasonable steps to avoid the commission of the offence.


(3\)Regulations may not be made by the Department under paragraph [(2\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04672)[(a)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04675) unless a draft of the regulations has been laid before and approved by a resolution of the Assembly.


(4\)A person guilty of an offence under this Article is liable on summary conviction to a fine not exceeding level 5 on the standard scale.”


Commencement Information

I98S. 80 in force at Royal Assent for specified purposes, see [**s. 175(2\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/2)

I99S. 80 in force at 29\.9\.2026 in so far as not already in force, see [**s. 175(1\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/1)

Prospective

#### 81Purchase of vaping or nicotine products on behalf of under 18s

(1\)The Health and Personal Social Services (Northern Ireland) Order 1978 ([S.I. 1978/1907 (N.I. 26\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/nisi/1978/1907)) is amended as follows.


(2\)After Article [4H](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04666) (inserted by section [80](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-80) of this Act) substitute—


##### “4IPurchase of vaping or nicotine products on behalf of under 18s

(1\)It is an offence for a person aged 18 or over to buy, or attempt to buy, a vaping product or nicotine product on behalf of a person who is under the age of 18\.


(2\)It is a defence for a person charged with an offence under this Article to prove that they had no reason to suspect that the other person was under the age of 18\.


(3\)A person guilty of an offence under this Article is liable on summary conviction to a fine not exceeding level 5 on the standard scale.”


(3\)In Article 4A (purchase of tobacco or nicotine products on behalf of persons under 18\)—


(a)in paragraph (1\), for “tobacco, cigarette papers or a relevant nicotine product” substitute “tobacco products, herbal smoking products or cigarette papers”;


(b)in the heading, for “or nicotine products” substitute “etc”.


Commencement Information

I100S. 81 in force at 29\.9\.2026, see [**s. 175(1\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/1)

Prospective

#### 82Vaping and nicotine product vending machines

After Article [4I](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04712) of the Health and Personal Social Services (Northern Ireland) Order 1978 ([S.I. 1978/1907 (N.I. 26\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/nisi/1978/1907)) (inserted by section [81](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-81) of this Act) insert—


##### “4JVaping and nicotine product vending machines

(1\)A person commits an offence if the person has the management or control of premises on which a vape vending machine or a nicotine product vending machine is available for use.


(2\)A person guilty of an offence under this Article is liable on summary conviction to a fine not exceeding level 5 on the standard scale.


(3\)In this Article—


<ul><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>nicotine product vending machine</span></span><span>” means a machine—</span>
</p><div><div><div><div>(a)</div><p><span>from which nicotine products may be bought, or</span>
</p></div><div><div>(b)</div><p><span>from which they are dispensed to a customer in connection with a sale;</span>
</p></div></div></div></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>vape vending machine</span></span><span>” means a machine—</span>
</p><div><div><div><div>(a)</div><p><span>from which vaping products may be bought, or</span>
</p></div><div><div>(b)</div><p><span>from which they are dispensed to a customer in connection with a sale.<span>”</span></span>
</p></div></div></div></li></ul>

Commencement Information

I101S. 82 in force at 29\.9\.2026, see [**s. 175(1\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/1)

### Displays of products or prices

#### 83Displays of products and prices in Northern Ireland

After Article [4J](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04750) of the Health and Personal Social Services (Northern Ireland) Order 1978 ([S.I. 1978/1907 (N.I. 26\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/nisi/1978/1907)) (inserted by section [82](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-82)) insert—


##### “Displays of products or prices

###### 4KDisplays of products or prices

(1\)The Department may by regulations impose prohibitions, requirements or limitations on retailers in relation to—


(a)the display, in the course of business, of relevant products in a place where those products are offered for sale;


(b)the display, in the course of business, of empty retail packaging of relevant products in a place where those products are offered for sale;


(c)the display, in the course of business, of prices of relevant products in a place where those products are offered for sale.


(2\)In paragraph [(1\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04804) “relevant product” means—


(a)tobacco products,


(b)tobacco related devices,


(c)herbal smoking products,


(d)cigarette papers,


(e)vaping products, or


(f)nicotine products.


(3\)In paragraph [(1\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04804)[(a)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04807) a reference to a product includes anything that represents the product and that is intended to be exchanged for it at the point of sale.


(4\)Regulations under paragraph [(1\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04804) may create offences in relation to a failure to comply with the regulations.


(5\)The regulations must provide for any offence to be triable on indictment or summarily and punishable—


(a)on summary conviction, by imprisonment for a term not exceeding 6 months, or a fine not exceeding the statutory maximum, or both;


(b)on conviction on indictment, by imprisonment for a term not exceeding 2 years, or a fine, or both.


(6\)Before making regulations under this Article the Department must consult any persons it considers it appropriate to consult.


(7\)Regulations may not be made by the Department under this Article unless a draft of the regulations has been laid before and approved by a resolution of the Assembly.”


Commencement Information

I102S. 83 in force at Royal Assent for specified purposes, see [**s. 175(2\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/2)

I103S. 83 in force at 29\.9\.2026 in so far as not already in force, see [**s. 175(1\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/1)

Prospective

### Free distribution and discounts

#### 84Free distribution and discount of products

After Article [4K](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04802) of the Health and Personal Social Services (Northern Ireland) Order 1978 ([S.I. 1978/1907 (N.I. 26\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/nisi/1978/1907)) (inserted by section [83](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-83)) insert—


##### “Free distribution and discounts

###### 4LFree distribution and discounts of products

(1\)A person commits an offence if—


(a)the person—


(i)gives away a product or coupon to a member of the public or sells a product or coupon at a substantial discount, or


(ii)causes or permits that to happen, and


(b)either—


(i)their purpose in doing so is to promote a relevant product, or


(ii)the effect of their doing so will be to promote a relevant product and they know, or have reason to suspect, that will be the effect.


(2\)In paragraph [(1\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04897) “relevant product” means—


(a)a tobacco product,


(b)a herbal smoking product,


(c)cigarette papers,


(d)a vaping product, or


(e)a nicotine product.


(3\)Where a person is charged with an offence under this Article of giving away a vaping product or nicotine product, or a coupon for such a product, it is a defence for the person to prove that the product or coupon was given away in accordance with arrangements made by a public authority.


(4\)A person guilty of an offence under this Article is liable—


(a)on summary conviction, to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 6 months, or a fine not exceeding the statutory maximum, or both;


(b)on conviction on indictment, to imprisonment for a term not exceeding 2 years, or a fine, or both.


(5\)In this Article “coupon” means anything (whether in physical or electronic form) which, by itself or together with something else, can be redeemed for a product or service or for cash or any other benefit.”


Commencement Information

I104S. 84 in force at 29\.9\.2026, see [**s. 175(1\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/1)

Prospective

### Enforcement

#### 85Programme of enforcement action by district councils

Before Article 7 of the Health and Personal Social Services (Northern Ireland) Order 1978 ([S.I. 1978/1907 (N.I. 26\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/nisi/1978/1907)) insert—


##### “Enforcement

###### 6AProgramme of enforcement action by district councils

(1\)Each district council must, at least once a year, consider—


(a)whether it is appropriate to carry out a programme of enforcement action in its area, and


(b)if so, what that programme should involve.


(2\)In paragraph [(1\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04985) “programme of enforcement action” means a programme involving one or more of the following—


(a)the investigation of complaints in respect of an alleged offence under—


(i)this Part or regulations under Article [4K](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04802), or


(ii)the Tobacco Retailers Act (Northern Ireland) 2014;


(b)the bringing of prosecutions in respect of such an offence;


(c)the taking of other measures intended to reduce the incidence of such offences.”


Commencement Information

I105S. 85 in force at 29\.9\.2026, see [**s. 175(1\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/1)

Prospective

### Interpretation of 1978 Order

#### 86Interpretation of 1978 Order

For Article 7 of the Health and Personal Social Services (Northern Ireland) Order 1978 ([S.I. 1978/1907 (N.I. 26\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/nisi/1978/1907)) substitute—


##### “Interpretation

###### 7Interpretation of Part 2

In this Part—


<ul><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>cigarette papers</span></span><span>” includes anything intended to be used for encasing tobacco products or herbal smoking products for the purpose of enabling them to be smoked;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>filter</span></span><span>” means a filter that is intended to be used when smoking a tobacco product or herbal smoking product (including a filter that forms part of, or that is intended to be inserted into, an item such as a cigarette holder or pipe);</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>herbal smoking product</span></span><span>” means a product consisting wholly or partly of vegetable matter and intended to be smoked but not containing tobacco;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>medical device</span></span><span>” has the meaning given by the Medical Devices Regulations 2002 (</span><a href="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/2002/618"><span>S.I. 2002/618</span></a><span>);</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>medicinal product</span></span><span>” has the meaning given by the Human Medicines Regulations 2012 (</span><a href="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/2012/1916"><span>S.I. 2012/1916</span></a><span>);</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>nicotine product</span></span><span>” has the meaning given by Article </span><a href="https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05143"><span>7A</span></a><span>;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>premises</span></span><span>” means any place (including a vehicle or moveable structure);</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>retail packaging</span></span><span>”, in relation to a thing, means the packaging in which it is, or is intended to be, presented for sale by retail;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>sell</span></span><span>” means sell by retail;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>tobacco product</span></span><span>” means a product consisting wholly or partly of tobacco and intended to be smoked, sniffed, sucked, chewed or consumed in any other way;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>tobacco related device</span></span><span>” means—</span>
</p><div><div><div><div>(a)</div><p><span>a device, other than a vape, which enables a tobacco product to be consumed (for example, a heated tobacco device or pipe), or</span>
</p></div><div><div>(b)</div><p><span>an item which is intended to form part of such a device;</span>
</p></div></div></div></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>tobacco retailer</span></span><span>” means a person who carries on a business involving the sale of tobacco products by retail;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>vape</span></span><span>” means—</span>
</p><div><div><div><div>(a)</div><p><span>a device which—</span>
</p><div><div><div><div>(i)</div><p><span>vaporises substances, other than tobacco, for the purpose of inhalation through a mouthpiece (whether or not it also vaporises tobacco), and</span>
</p></div><div><div>(ii)</div><p><span>is not a medical device or a medicinal product, or</span>
</p></div></div></div></div><div><div>(b)</div><p><span>an item which is intended to form part of a device within paragraph </span><a href="https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05100"><span>(a)</span></a><span> (including anything intended to be attached to it with a view to imparting flavour);</span>
</p></div></div></div></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>vaping product</span></span><span>” means—</span>
</p><div><div><div><div>(a)</div><p><span>a vape, or</span>
</p></div><div><div>(b)</div><p><span>a vaping substance;</span>
</p></div></div></div></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>vaping substance</span></span><span>” means a substance, other than tobacco, that is intended to be vaporised by a vape;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>vaporises</span></span><span>” includes aerosolises;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>vehicle</span></span><span>” means every type of vehicle, including a vessel, aircraft and hovercraft.</span>
</p></li></ul>

###### 7AMeaning of nicotine product

(1\)In this Part “nicotine product” means—


(a)a device which is intended to enable nicotine to be delivered into the human body,


(b)an item which is intended to form part of a device within sub\-paragraph [(a)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05148),


(c)nicotine, or any substance containing nicotine, which is intended to be delivered into the human body, or


(d)an item containing anything within sub\-paragraph [(c)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05157).


(2\)But the following are not “nicotine products” for the purposes of this Article—


(a)a tobacco product;


(b)a herbal smoking product;


(c)cigarette papers;


(d)any device which is intended to be used for the consumption of tobacco products;


(e)a vaping product;


(f)a medical device;


(g)a medicinal product.”


Commencement Information

I106S. 86 in force at 29\.9\.2026, see [**s. 175(1\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/1)

### Retailer register and licensing

Prospective

#### 87Extension of retailer register

Commencement Information

I107S. 87 not in force at Royal Assent, see [**s. 175(8\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/8)

#### 88Prohibition of retail sales of tobacco products etc without a licence

(1\)After [section 4](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/nia/2014/4/section/4) of the [Tobacco Retailers Act (Northern Ireland) 2014](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/nia/2014/4/contents) (c. 4 (N.I.)) insert—


##### “Licensing of retail sales of tobacco products etc

###### 4AProhibition of retail sales of tobacco products etc without a licence

(1\)An individual must not do any of the following things except under the authority of and in accordance with a personal licence—


(a)sell relevant products;


(b)expose relevant products for sale;


(c)possess relevant products for the purpose of their sale (by the individual or another person).


(2\)A person must not use or permit the use of premises for any of the following things except under the authority of and in accordance with a premises licence—


(a)the storage of relevant products for the purpose of their sale (by the person or another person);


(b)the exposure of relevant products for sale;


(c)the supply of relevant products to retail customers.


(3\)Regulations may create exceptions to the prohibition in subsection [(1\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05224) or [(2\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05240).


(4\)Regulations must make provision for and in connection with the grant of personal licences and premises licences.


(5\)Before making regulations under this section the Department must consult any persons the Department considers it appropriate to consult.


(6\)Schedule 1 makes further provision about regulations under [subsection (4\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05262).


(7\)In this section—


<ul><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>grant</span></span><span>” includes variation or renewal;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>licensing authority</span></span><span>” has the meaning given by paragraph 2 of Schedule 1;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>personal licence</span></span><span>” means a licence that is granted by a licensing authority and authorises an individual to do the things mentioned in subsection </span><a href="https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05224"><span>(1)</span></a><a href="https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05227"><span>(a)</span></a><span>, </span><a href="https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05231"><span>(b)</span></a><span> and </span><a href="https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05235"><span>(c)</span></a><span>;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>premises licence</span></span><span>” means a licence that is granted by a licensing authority and authorises the use of premises by a person for the things mentioned in subsection </span><a href="https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05240"><span>(2)</span></a><a href="https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05243"><span>(a)</span></a><span>, </span><a href="https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05247"><span>(b)</span></a><span> and </span><a href="https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05251"><span>(c)</span></a><span>;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>relevant products</span></span><span>” means—</span>
</p><div><div><div><div>(a)</div><p><span>tobacco products;</span>
</p></div><div><div>(b)</div><p><span>herbal smoking products;</span>
</p></div><div><div>(c)</div><p><span>cigarette papers;</span>
</p></div><div><div>(d)</div><p><span>vaping products;</span>
</p></div><div><div>(e)</div><p><span>nicotine products;</span>
</p></div></div></div></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>sell</span></span><span>” means sell by retail;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>supply</span></span><span>” includes despatch.</span>
</p></li></ul>

###### 4BOffences in connection with licences

(1\)A person who breaches the prohibition in [section 4A](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05222)[(1\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05224) or [(2\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05240) commits an offence.


(2\)A person commits an offence if—


(a)the person provides information to a licensing authority—


(i)in, or in connection with, an application for the grant of a personal licence or a premises licence, or


(ii)in pursuance of any other obligation imposed by or under regulations made under [section 4A](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05222)[(4\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05262),


(b)the information is false or misleading in a material respect, and


(c)the person knows, or ought reasonably to know, that the information is false or misleading in a material respect.


(3\)A person who commits an offence under this section is liable on summary conviction to a fine not exceeding level 5 on the standard scale.


(4\)The court by which a person is convicted of an offence under subsection (1\) may order the relevant products to which the offence relates, and any container for them, to be forfeited and either destroyed or dealt with in such other manner as the court may order.


(5\)In this section—


<ul><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>grant</span></span><span>” includes variation or renewal;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>licensing authority</span></span><span>” has the meaning given by paragraph 2 of Schedule 1;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>personal licence</span></span><span>” has the meaning given by </span><a href="https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05222"><span>section 4A</span></a><a href="https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05275"><span>(7)</span></a><span>;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>premises licence</span></span><span>” has the meaning given by </span><a href="https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05222"><span>section 4A</span></a><a href="https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05275"><span>(7)</span></a><span>;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>relevant product</span></span><span>” has the meaning given by </span><a href="https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05222"><span>section 4A</span></a><a href="https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05275"><span>(7)</span></a><span>.</span>
</p></li></ul>

###### 4CFinancial penalties for breach of licence conditions

(1\)A council may impose a financial penalty on a person if satisfied that—


(a)the person has breached a condition attached to a personal licence or a premises licence, and


(b)the breach of that condition does not constitute an offence under section 4B.


(2\)The amount of the financial penalty must not exceed £2,500\.


(3\)Regulations may amend the amount specified in subsection (2\) for the purpose of reflecting inflation.


(4\)Schedule 2 makes further provision about the imposition of financial penalties under this section.


(5\)In this section “personal licence” and “premises licence” have the meaning given by [section 4A](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05222)[(7\)](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05275).”


(2\)[Schedule 11](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#schedule-11) inserts new [Schedule 1](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/nia/2014/4/schedule/1) to the [Tobacco Retailers Act (Northern Ireland) 2014](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/nia/2014/4/contents), relating to the grant of personal licences and premises licences.


(3\)[Schedule 12](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#schedule-12) inserts new [Schedule 2](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/nia/2014/4/schedule/2) to the [Tobacco Retailers Act (Northern Ireland) 2014](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/nia/2014/4/contents), relating to the imposition of financial penalties.


(4\)[Schedule 13](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#schedule-13) contains consequential amendments relating to the licensing of retail sales of tobacco products etc.


Commencement Information

I108S. 88 in force at Royal Assent for specified purposes, see [**s. 175(2\)(8\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/2/8)

### Powers to extend legislation

#### 89Power to extend legislation to other products

(1\)After Article [6A](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04983) of the Health and Personal Social Services (Northern Ireland) Order 1978 ([S.I. 1978/1907 (N.I. 26\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/nisi/1978/1907)) (inserted by section [85](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#section-85) of this Act) insert—


##### “Power to extend this Part

###### 6BPower to extend this Part to other products

(1\)The Department may by regulations amend this Part for the purpose of extending any provision that applies in relation to a tobacco product to—


(a)a filter that does not form part of a tobacco product or herbal smoking product;


(b)a tobacco related device.


(2\)The Department may by regulations amend this Part for the purpose of extending to filters any provision made by Articles [4E](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04532) to [4G](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p04627) in relation to a relevant oral tobacco product.


(3\)Before making regulations under this Article the Department must consult any persons it considers it appropriate to consult.


(4\)Regulations may not be made by the Department under this Article unless a draft of the regulations has been laid before and approved by a resolution of the Assembly.”


(2\)After section 21 of the Tobacco Retailers Act (Northern Ireland) [2014 (c. 4 (N.I.))](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/nia/2014/4) insert—


##### “21APower to extend Act to other products

(1\)The Department may by regulations amend this Act for the purpose of extending any provision that applies in relation to a tobacco product to—


(a)a filter that does not form part of a tobacco product or herbal smoking product;


(b)a device of a specified description which enables a tobacco product to be consumed (for example, a heated tobacco device or pipe);


(c)an item which is intended to form part of such a device.


(2\)Before making regulations under this section the Department must consult any persons the Department considers it appropriate to consult.”


(3\)In section 24 of that Act, in subsection (2\), for “or 21(4\) or (5\)” substitute “, 21(4\) or (5\) or [21A](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p05525)”.


Commencement Information

I109S. 89 in force at Royal Assent for specified purposes, see [**s. 175(2\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/2)

I110S. 89 in force at 29\.9\.2026 in so far as not already in force, see [**s. 175(1\)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/175/1)

(2\)See Schedule [15](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#schedule-15) for consequential amendments coming into force on 1 January 2027\.
