Schedule 17Amendments consequential on sections 142 to 146
----------------------------------------------------------

1The Health Act 2006 is amended as follows.

Commencement Information

I408Sch. 17 para. 1 not in force at Royal Assent, see [**s. 176(3\)(a)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/176/3/a)

2(1\)Section 2 is amended as follows.

(2\)For subsection (2\) substitute—

“(2\)Premises in England are smoke\-free if they are workplaces; they are smoke\-free all the time.”


(3\)In subsection (3\), for “used as a place of work mentioned in subsection (2\)” substitute “a workplace”.

(4\)For subsections (7\) and (8\) substitute—

“(7\)In this Part “workplace” means—


(a)a place of work used by more than one person (even if the persons who work there do so at different times, or only intermittently), or


(b)a place of work where members of the public might attend for the purpose of seeking or receiving goods or services from the person or persons working there (even if members of the public are not always present).”


Commencement Information

### “Dehongli

#### 17ADehongli’r Bennod hon

(1\)Yn y Bennod hon—


<ul><li><p><span>ystyr “</span><span><span>cartref gofal i oedolion</span></span><span>” (“</span><em><span>adult care home</span></em><span>”) yw mangre lle y darperir gwasanaeth cartref gofal o fewn yr ystyr a roddir gan baragraff 1 o Atodlen 1 i Ddeddf Rheoleiddio ac Arolygu Gofal Cymdeithasol (Cymru) </span><a href="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/anaw/2016/2"><span>2016 (dccc 2)</span></a><span> i bersonau sy’n 18 oed neu’n hŷn;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>mae “</span><span><span>cerbyd</span></span><span>” (“</span><em><span>vehicle</span></em><span>”) yn cynnwys trên, tram, cwch neu long, hofrenfad ac awyren;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>mae “</span><span><span>cyfarpar maes chwarae</span></span><span>” (“</span><em><span>playground equipment</span></em><span>”) yn cynnwys (er enghraifft) siglen, llithren, pwll tywod, neu ramp, ond nid yw’n cynnwys cyfarpar â modur (megis cyfarpar sy’n rhedeg ar fodur trydanol);</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>mae i “</span><span><span>Cymru</span></span><span>” yr ystyr a roddir i “Wales” gan adran 158(1) o Ddeddf Llywodraeth Cymru </span><a href="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2006/32"><span>2006 (p.32)</span></a><span>;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>mae i “</span><span><span>disgybl cofrestredig</span></span><span>” yr ystyr a roddir i “registered pupil” gan adran 434(5) o Ddeddf Addysg </span><a href="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/1996/56"><span>1996 (p.56)</span></a><span>;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>ystyr “</span><span><span>gofal plant</span></span><span>” (“</span><em><span>childcare</span></em><span>”) yw (yn ddarostyngedig i is-adran (2)) unrhyw ffurf ar ofal ar gyfer plentyn, ac eithrio gofal a ddarperir ar gyfer plentyn gan riant, perthynas neu riant maeth i’r plentyn, ac mae’n cynnwys—</span>
</p><div><div><div><div>(a)</div><p><span>addysg ar gyfer plentyn, a</span>
</p></div><div><div>(b)</div><p><span>unrhyw weithgaredd arall o dan oruchwyliaeth ar gyfer plentyn;</span>
</p></div></div></div></li><li><p><span>ystyr “</span><span><span>hosbis i oedolion</span></span><span>” (“</span><em><span>adult hospice</span></em><span>”) yw mangre a ddefnyddir yn gyfan gwbl neu’n bennaf ar gyfer darparu gofal lliniarol i bersonau sy’n 18 oed neu’n hŷn, sy’n dioddef o glefyd sy’n gwaethygu ac sydd yn ei gyfnodau olaf, gan neu ar ran sefydliad â’i brif swyddogaeth yw darparu gofal o’r fath;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>mae “</span><span><span>mangre</span></span><span>” (“</span><em><span>premises</span></em><span>”) yn cynnwys—</span>
</p><div><div><div><div>(a)</div><p><span>unrhyw fan;</span>
</p></div><div><div>(b)</div><p><span>strwythur symudol ac eithrio cerbyd;</span>
</p></div><div><div>(c)</div><p><span>stondin;</span>
</p></div><div><div>(d)</div><p><span>pabell;</span>
</p></div><div><div>(e)</div><p><span>gosodiad alltraeth o fewn yr ystyr a roddir i “offshore installation” yn Neddf Gweithiau Mwynau (Gosodiadau Alltraeth) </span><a href="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/1971/61"><span>1971 (p.61)</span></a><span> (gweler adran 12 o’r Ddeddf honno);</span>
</p></div></div></div></li><li><p><span>ystyr “</span><span><span>perthynas</span></span><span>” (“</span><em><span>relative</span></em><span>”), mewn perthynas â phlentyn, yw llys-riant, mam-gu/nain, tad-cu/taid, modryb, ewythr, brawd neu chwaer (gan gynnwys unrhyw berson sydd yn y berthynas honno yn rhinwedd priodas neu bartneriaeth sifil neu berthynas deuluol barhaus);</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>ystyr “</span><span><span>plentyn</span></span><span>” (“</span><em><span>child</span></em><span>”) yw person o dan 18 oed;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>mae “</span><span><span>rhiant</span></span><span>” (“</span><em><span>parent</span></em><span>”) yn cynnwys unrhyw berson a chanddo gyfrifoldeb rhiant (o fewn yr ystyr a roddir i “parental responsibility” yn adran 3 o Ddeddf Plant </span><a href="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/1989/41"><span>1989 (p.41)</span></a><span>) dros blentyn;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>mae i “</span><span><span>ysbyty</span></span><span>” yr ystyr a roddir i “hospital” gan adran 206 o Ddeddf y Gwasanaeth Iechyd Gwladol (Cymru) </span><a href="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2006/42"><span>2006 (p.42)</span></a><span>;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>mae i “</span><span><span>ysgol</span></span><span>” yr ystyr a roddir i “</span><em><span>school</span></em><span>” gan adran 4 o Ddeddf Addysg </span><a href="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/1996/56"><span>1996 (p.56)</span></a><span>;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>mae “</span><span><span>ysmygu</span></span><span>” (“</span><em><span>smoking</span></em><span>” a “</span><em><span>smokes</span></em><span>”) i gael ei ddarllen yn unol ag adran 4.</span>
</p></li></ul>

(2\)Nid yw cyfeiriadau yn y Bennod hon at “gofal plant” yn cynnwys—


(a)addysg (neu unrhyw weithgaredd arall o dan oruchwyliaeth) a ddarperir gan ysgol yn ystod oriau ysgol ar gyfer disgybl cofrestredig, na


(b)unrhyw ffurf ar ofal iechyd ar gyfer plentyn.


(3\)At ddibenion is\-adran (1\) mae person yn rhiant maeth mewn perthynas â phlentyn os yw’r person—


(a)yn rhiant maeth awdurdod lleol (o fewn yr ystyr a roddir gan adran 197 o Ddeddf Gwasanaethau Cymdeithasol a Llesiant (Cymru) [2014 (dccc 4\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/anaw/2014/4)), neu


(b)yn maethu’r plentyn yn breifat.


(4\)Mae cyfeiriadau yn y Bennod hon at “annedd” yn cynnwys tir a fwynheir gyda mangre pan fo’r fangre ei hun yn annedd, oni bai bod y tir yn dir amaethyddol (o fewn yr ystyr a roddir gan adran 246 o Ddeddf Rhentu Cartrefi (Cymru) [2016 (dccc 1\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/anaw/2016/1)) sy’n fwy na 0\.809 hectar.


(5\)Mae cyfeiriadau yn y Bennod hon, sut bynnag y’u mynegir, at fangreoedd neu gerbydau sy’n ddi\-fwg (neu nad ydynt yn ddi\-fwg) (neu sy’n cael eu trin fel pe baent yn ddi\-fwg) yn gyfeiriadau at y mangreoedd hynny neu’r cerbydau hynny i’r graddau y maent yn ddi\-fwg (neu nad ydynt yn ddi\-fwg) (neu’n cael eu trin fel pe baent yn ddi\-fwg) o dan y Bennod hon neu yn rhinwedd y Bennod hon.


(6\)Gall mangreoedd fod yn ddi\-fwg yn rhinwedd mwy nag un adran yn y Bennod hon.


(7\)Caiff rheoliadau bennu at ddiben y Bennod hon ystyr “caeedig”, “sylweddol gaeedig” ac “nad yw’n gaeedig nac yn sylweddol gaeedig.”

3In the English language text, after section 17 insert—

### “Interpretation

#### 17AInterpretation of this Chapter

(1\)In this Chapter—


<ul><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>adult care home</span></span><span>” (“</span><span><em><span>cartref gofal i oedolion</span></em></span><span>”) means premises at which a care home service within the meaning given by paragraph 1 of Schedule 1 to the Regulation and Inspection of Social Care (Wales) Act </span><a href="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/anaw/2016/2"><span>2016 (anaw 2)</span></a><span> is provided to persons aged 18 or over;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>adult hospice</span></span><span>” (“</span><span><em><span>hosbis i oedolion</span></em></span><span>”) means premises wholly or mainly used for the provision of palliative care to persons aged 18 or over, who are suffering from a progressive disease in its final stages, by or behalf of an establishment the primary function of which is the provision of such care;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>child</span></span><span>” (“</span><span><em><span>plentyn</span></em></span><span>”) means a person aged under 18;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>childcare</span></span><span>” (“</span><span><em><span>gofal plant</span></em></span><span>”) means (subject to subsection (2)) any form of care for a child, other than care provided for a child by a parent, relative or foster parent of the child, and includes—</span>
</p><div><div><div><div>(a)</div><p><span>education for a child, and</span>
</p></div><div><div>(b)</div><p><span>any other supervised activity for a child;</span>
</p></div></div></div></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>hospital</span></span><span>” (“</span><span><em><span>ysbyty</span></em></span><span>”) has the meaning given by section 206 of the National Health Service (Wales) Act </span><a href="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2006/42"><span>2006 (c.42)</span></a><span>;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>parent</span></span><span>” (“</span><span><em><span>rhiant</span></em></span><span>”) includes any person who has parental responsibility (within the meaning of section 3 of the Children Act </span><a href="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/1989/41"><span>1989 (c.41)</span></a><span>) for a child;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>playground equipment</span></span><span>” (“</span><span><em><span>cyfarpar maes chwarae</span></em></span><span>”) includes (for example) a swing, slide, sand-pit, or ramp, but does not include powered equipment (such as equipment powered by electric motor);</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>premises</span></span><span>” (“</span><span><em><span>mangre</span></em></span><span>”) includes—</span>
</p><div><div><div><div>(a)</div><p><span>any place;</span>
</p></div><div><div>(b)</div><p><span>a moveable structure other than a vehicle;</span>
</p></div><div><div>(c)</div><p><span>a stall;</span>
</p></div><div><div>(d)</div><p><span>a tent;</span>
</p></div><div><div>(e)</div><p><span>an offshore installation within the meaning given in the Mineral Workings (Offshore Installations) Act </span><a href="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/1971/61"><span>1971 (c.61)</span></a><span> (see section 12 of that Act);</span>
</p></div></div></div></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>registered pupil</span></span><span>” (“</span><span><em><span>disgybl cofrestredig</span></em></span><span>”) has the meaning given by section 434(5) of the Education Act </span><a href="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/1996/56"><span>1996 (c.56)</span></a><span>;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>relative</span></span><span>” (“</span><span><em><span>perthynas</span></em></span><span>”), in relation to a child, means a step-parent, grandparent, aunt, uncle, brother or sister (including any person who is in that relationship by virtue of a marriage or civil partnership or an enduring family relationship);</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>school</span></span><span>” (“</span><span><em><span>ysgol</span></em></span><span>”) has the meaning given by section 4 of the Education Act </span><a href="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/1996/56"><span>1996 (c.56)</span></a><span>;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“smoking” and “</span><span><span>smokes</span></span><span>” (“</span><span><em><span>ysmygu</span></em></span><span>”) are to be read in accordance with section 4;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>vehicle</span></span><span>” (“</span><span><em><span>cerbyd</span></em></span><span>”) includes a train, tram, vessel, hovercraft and aircraft;</span>
</p></li><li><p><span>“</span><span><span>Wales</span></span><span>” (“</span><span><em><span>Cymru</span></em></span><span>”) has the meaning given by section 158(1) of the Government of Wales Act </span><a href="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2006/32"><span>2006 (c.32)</span></a><span>.</span>
</p></li></ul>

(2\)References in this Chapter to “childcare” do not include—


(a)education (or any other supervised activity) provided by a school during school hours for a registered pupil, or


(b)any form of health care for a child.


(3\)For the purposes of subsection (1\) a person is a foster parent in relation to a child if the person—


(a)is a local authority foster parent (within the meaning given by section 197 of the Social Services and Well\-being (Wales) Act [2014 (anaw 4\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/anaw/2014/4)), or


(b)fosters the child privately.


(4\)References in this Chapter to a “dwelling” include land enjoyed with premises where the premises themselves constitute a dwelling, unless the land is agricultural land (within the meaning given by section 246 of the Renting Homes (Wales) Act [2016 (anaw 1\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/anaw/2016/1)) exceeding 0\.809 hectares.


(5\)References in this Chapter, however expressed, to premises or vehicles which are (or are not) smoke\-free (or treated as smoke\-free), are to those premises or vehicles so far as they are (or are not) smoke\-free (or treated as smoke\-free) under or by virtue of this Chapter.


(6\)Premises may be smoke\-free by virtue of more than one section in this Chapter.


(7\)Regulations may specify for the purpose of this Chapter what “enclosed”, “substantially enclosed” and “not enclosed or substantially enclosed” mean.”

### Smoking (Northern Ireland) Order 2006 ([S.I. 2006/2957 (N.I. 20\)](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/nisi/2006/2957))

1The Smoking (Northern Ireland) Order 2006 is amended as follows.


Commencement Information

I448Sch. 20 para. 1 not in force at Royal Assent, see [**s. 176(3\)(d)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/176/3/d)

2In Article 2, in paragraph (3\), at the appropriate places insert—

<ul><li><p><span><span>“</span>“</span><span><span>heated tobacco device</span></span><span>” means a device that heats tobacco to generate a vapour or an aerosol for the purpose of inhalation through a mouthpiece (whether or not it can also heat other matter to produce a vapour or aerosol);<span>”</span>;</span>
</p></li></ul>

<ul><li><p><span><span>“</span>“</span><span><span>open to the public</span></span><span>”: premises and places are open to the public if the public or a section of the public has access to them, whether by invitation or not, and whether on payment or not;<span>”</span>;</span>
</p></li></ul>

<ul><li><p><span><span>“</span>“</span><span><span>performance</span></span><span>” includes—</span>
</p><div><div><div><div>(a)</div><p><span>the performance of a play or a performance given in connection with the making of a film or television programme, and</span>
</p></div><div><div>(b)</div><p><span>a rehearsal;<span>”</span>;</span>
</p></div></div></div></li></ul>

<ul><li><p><span><span>“</span>“</span><span><span>relevant vape</span></span><span>” means a vape that is not a heated tobacco device;<span>”</span>;</span>
</p></li></ul>

<ul><li><p><span><span>“</span>“</span><span><span>vape</span></span><span>” has the meaning given by Article 7 of the Health and Personal Social Services (Northern Ireland) Order 1978;<span>”</span>;</span>
</p></li></ul>

<ul><li><p><span><span>“</span>“</span><span><span>vaporises</span></span><span>” has the meaning given by Article 7 of the Health and Personal Social Services (Northern Ireland) Order 1978;<span>”</span>;</span>
</p></li></ul>

<ul><li><p><span><span>“</span>“</span><span><span>workplace</span></span><span>” has the meaning given by Article 3</span><a href="https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2026/18/data.xht#p17723"><span>(7)</span></a><span>;<span>”</span>.</span>
</p></li></ul>

Commencement Information

I449Sch. 20 para. 2 not in force at Royal Assent, see [**s. 176(3\)(d)**](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/ukpga/2026/18/section/176/3/d)

3(1\)Article 3 is amended as follows.


(2\)For paragraph (2\) substitute—


“(2\)Premises are smoke\-free if they are workplaces; they are smoke\-free all the time.”


(3\)In paragraph (3\), for “used as a place of work mentioned in paragraph (2\)” substitute “a workplace”.


(4\)For paragraph (7\) substitute—


“(7\)In this Order “workplace” means—


(a)a place of work used by more than one person (even if the persons who work there do so at different times, or only intermittently), or


(b)a place of work where members of the public might attend for the purpose of seeking or receiving goods or services from the person or persons working there (even if members of the public are not always present).”
